    y = 13

        x = -1
        y = -9

            check_variable = {
                var = PRC_49_60_focus_var

                compare = equals
            }
        }
    }

        NOT = {

				var = PRC_focus_tree_var

				compare = not_equals
			}

                value = 2
                compare = not_equals
            }

        always = no

            country_event = {

            }
